if (!is_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf') != '036ec70355b29ad22e6cf87bc7f0e650d4055428') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf') !== '036ec70355b29ad22e6cf87bc7f0e650d4055428') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf') !== '95b72a2b9ce760ffd24dccd2103e69832ddf3a82') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf') !== '036ec70355b29ad22e6cf87bc7f0e650d4055428') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') != '55ff13ce4463305c7df2e7bf6f13e4d5adfb663d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== '55ff13ce4463305c7df2e7bf6f13e4d5adfb663d') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== '4afb600eb0c2b6a1b0cc04e769f31708bc73009e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== '55ff13ce4463305c7df2e7bf6f13e4d5adfb663d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') != '5b0d4ac34e0995dc86650333df53cd0a28c5f093') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '5b0d4ac34e0995dc86650333df53cd0a28c5f093') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '5b0d4ac34e0995dc86650333df53cd0a28c5f093') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');

	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') != 'f557c37c9955e18f899da81771f9be8afd654308') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== 'f557c37c9955e18f899da81771f9be8afd654308') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== 'd1a588fe466e9b92de266f7c5e171fc8114a5bb5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== 'f557c37c9955e18f899da81771f9be8afd654308') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') != '8c1b06c9fbac02e901d94eb7a2f151da2286889d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== '8c1b06c9fbac02e901d94eb7a2f151da2286889d') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'be039560f844c7bee8c15381f230d1abae55c6da') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== '8c1b06c9fbac02e901d94eb7a2f151da2286889d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') != 'de4b742c6e984e57d20f9beb3f3502bcc3202b2b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/xml_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') !== 'de4b742c6e984e57d20f9beb3f3502bcc3202b2b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') !== '6e09c26bfbfd355b8d86468c51b30f197dbfa3d9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/xml_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/xml_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') !== 'de4b742c6e984e57d20f9beb3f3502bcc3202b2b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/check.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/check.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('update/check.php') !== '069e04a969e38d6d90308ccd489a02eb45fe762b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/check.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 499\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 499') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
